     function shiftPanes(e) { if ("back" == e && menuPage > 0) var a = -(100 * menuPage - 100); else var a = -(100 * menuPage); menuPanes.animate({ left: a + "%" }) } function hideMobileMenu() { var e = $("a#menu-button"); e.removeClass("active"), navMenu.removeClass("active"), contentWrap.removeClass("push"), menuShade.hide(), menuPanes.animate({ left: 0 }), navMenu.scrollTop(0), menuPanes.scrollTop(0), menuPage = 1 } var Viewport = $(window).width(), theMenu = $("div#mobile-header").detach(), searchContainer = $("#mobile-search").detach(); $("body div.w2").prepend(theMenu), theMenu.after(searchContainer); if ($("body").hasClass("mobile") && 500 >= Viewport || $("body").hasClass("Firefox") && 500 >= Viewport) { var navContainer = $("ul#nav"); $("ul#nav li.top-node").each(function () { var e = $(this).children("a.subfolderstyle"), a = e.clone(), n = $(this).find("div.drop"); n.prepend(a); var i = $(this).find("div.drop a.subfolderstyle"), t = i.text(), s = "View All " + t; i.text(s), i.addClass("to-hierarchy"), i.removeClass("subfolderstyle") }), $("div.drop div.col strong.title").each(function () { var e = $(this).html(), a = $(this).next("ul"); a.length > 0 ? $(this).addClass("has-links") : $(this).addClass("hyperlink"), a.addClass("link-list"), a.prepend(e); var n = a.find("a").first(); n.addClass("top-level"); var i = n.text(), t = "View All " + i; n.text(t) }), $("div#empty").each(function () { $(this).remove() }); var menuBar = $("div#mobile-header"), navMenu = $("div#mobile-menu-holder"), menuShade = $("div#mobile-menu-shade"), contentWrap = $("div#wrapper"), menuPanes = $("div#menu-panes"), searchText = $("span.searchText"), searchBox = $("#header div.search-from"), searchInput = searchBox.find('input[type="text"]'), searchSubmit = searchBox.find('input[type="submit"]'), firstPane = menuPanes.find("div.menu-pane").first(), mainMenu = $("ul#nav").clone(); firstPane.append(mainMenu); var utilityNav = $("ul#mobile-utility-buttons").detach(); navMenu.prepend(utilityNav), menuSearch = searchBox.detach(), searchContainer.append(menuSearch); var newAndClearance = '<li class="no-children"><a href="/New">New Items</a></li><li class="no-children"><a href="/Gifts">Gift Ideas</a></li><li class="no-children"><a href="/Closeouts">Closeouts</a></li>'; mainMenu.append(newAndClearance) } var menuPage = 1; $("div.menu-pane ul#nav li.top-node a").click(function (e) { var a = $(this).parent().parent().parent().next(".menu-pane"), n = a.find("div.the-menu"); n.empty(); var i = $(this).siblings("div").children(), t = i.clone(), s = $(this).text(), r = a.find("a.go-back"); r.text(s), n.append(t), shiftPanes("forward"), menuPage++, e.preventDefault() }), $("div.menu-pane div.the-menu").on("click", "strong.has-links a", function () { var e = $(this).closest(".menu-pane").next(".menu-pane"), a = e.find("div.the-menu"); a.empty(); var n = (e.parent(), $(this).text()), i = e.find("a.go-back"); i.text(n); var t = $(this).parent().next("ul.link-list"), s = t.clone(); return a.append(s), shiftPanes("forward"), menuPage++, menuPanes.scrollTop(0), !1 }), $("ul#mobile-utility-buttons li a, ul#nav li.no-children a").click(function () { return "call-button" == $(this).attr("id") ? !0 : (hideMobileMenu(), $("div#loading-overlay").show(), !0) }), $("div.menu-pane div.the-menu").on("click", "strong.hyperlink a, ul.link-list li a, a.to-hierarchy, a.top-level", function () { return hideMobileMenu(), $("div#loading-overlay").show(), !0 }), $("a.go-back").on("click", function () { return menuPage--, shiftPanes("back"), !1 }), $("a#menu-button").click(function () { return $(this).hasClass("active") ? hideMobileMenu() : ($(this).addClass("active"), navMenu.addClass("active"), contentWrap.addClass("push"), menuShade.show()), !1 }), $("div#mobile-menu-shade").click(function () { hideMobileMenu() });
